Comment: socapsu said "Spoken Peayce's purpose is to create a community through the foundation of the love we share for poetry. We are here to not only promote and raise awareness of the growing spoken word community, but also encourage free self-expression amongst peers. In doing so, we intend to empower and push one another to shoot higher than ours and others set expectations. Spoken Peayce is an organization that will strive to advertise both the group and each individual for the sake of perfecting our craft and sharing the gift of spoken word to friends, family, faculty, and students. Past events that they have helped with is Peay's Got Talent. Their meeting times are every Tuesday at 6pm , Clement Room 137
President:Christalynn Hamer
Advisor:Kenneth Cervelli
